if (!is_file('TODO')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: TODO');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('TODO')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != '6cbfbd2c06726f3d89f253043e0e3aa82128a08d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '6cbfbd2c06726f3d89f253043e0e3aa82128a08d') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5cda9ac47ed23de706817afd6c6d6cdf5ae87b0c') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '6cbfbd2c06726f3d89f253043e0e3aa82128a08d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/config_values.txt');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('doc/config_values.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') != 'f65990953d8ed149bc03b18772ceb5ee1bfde2fc') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/config_values.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/config_values.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'f65990953d8ed149bc03b18772ceb5ee1bfde2fc') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'a7ebc345ed9366f0d5a7d7f6bdecd686def140f5') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/config_values.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/config_values.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/config_values.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/config_values.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/config_values.txt') !== 'f65990953d8ed149bc03b18772ceb5ee1bfde2fc') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/config_values.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.min.js.php');
	writefile_27();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') != 'ed5e3fe4d958022e8ab0d5bb6bc1cb8bb2baedaa') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== 'ed5e3fe4d958022e8ab0d5bb6bc1cb8bb2baedaa') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== '7605cfb6edfab3142556aa487b5de06d6411d351') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_27();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== 'ed5e3fe4d958022e8ab0d5bb6bc1cb8bb2baedaa') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 1036\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 1036') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3
